2

一再的拖延打乱了全部安排。
yī zài de tuō yán dǎ luàn le quán bù ān pái。
The delays put the whole schedule out of joint.

一架飞机在机场着陆。
yī jià fēi jī zài jī chǎng zhuó lù。
An airplane alighted on the airdrome.

一般人都相信努力是值得的。
yī bān rén dōu xiāng xìn nǔ lì shì zhí de de。
It is generally believed that it pays to work hard.

一阵大风吹来，把门关上了。
yī zhèn dà fēng chuī lái， bǎ mén guān shàng le。
A gust of wind blew the door shut.

下一次邮递时间是四点钟。
xià yī cì yóu dì shí jiān shì sì diǎn zhōng。
The next postal delivery is at 4 o'clock.

下课铃响了.
xià kè líng xiǎng le.
There's the bell for the end of the lesson.

不用说，夏日的傍晚是多么美。
bù yòng shuō， xià rì de bàng wǎn shì duō me měi。
Needs not say how lovely are the summer evenings.

不系保险带开车就太傻了。
bù xì bǎo xiǎn dài kāi chē jiù tài shǎ le。
It's silly to drive without fastening one's seat belt.

两块田之间有一条树木带。
liǎng kuài tián zhī jiān yǒu yī tiáo shù mù dài。
A belt of trees grew between the two fields.

中国是一个原油丰富的国家。
Zhōng guó shì yī gè yuán yóu fēng fù de guó jiā。
China is a country rich in crude oil.

主席的讲话将向全国广播。
zhǔ xí de jiǎng huà jiàng xiàng quán guó guǎng bō。
The chairman's speech will be broadcast nationwide.

乘飞机旅行前他紧张不安。
chéng fēi jī lu:3 xíng qián tā jǐn zhāng bù ān。
He was nervous before the plane trip.

乡村生活确实让人愉快。
xiāng cūn shēng huó què shí ràng rén yú kuài。
Life in the country is rather delightful.

二十市斤折合十公斤。
èr shí shì jīn zhé hé shí gōng jīn。
20 jin goes to 10 kilograms.

云层正在堆积。
yún céng zhèng zài duī jī。
Clouds are banking up.

云层的构成方式有好几种。
yún céng de gòu chéng fāng shì yǒu hǎo jǐ zhòng。
There are several kinds of cloud formations.

人们叫她泼妇。
rén men jiào tā pō fù。
People called her shrew.

人们正排队买票。
rén men zhèng pái duì mǎi piào。
People are queuing to buy tickets.

从前有个美丽的公主....
cóng qián yǒu gè měi lì de gōng zhǔ....
Once upon a time there was a beautiful princess...

他一紧张就结巴。
tā yī jǐn zhāng jiù jié bā。
He stammers when he feels nervous.

他上午十一点才醒。
tā shàng wǔ shí yī diǎn cái xǐng。
He didn't wake up until 11 o'clock in the morning.

他不赞成改变党的方针。
tā bù zàn chéng gǎi biàn dǎng de fāng zhēn。
He deprecates changing the party's policy.

他主持修建这座桥的建筑工程。
tā zhǔ chí xiū jiàn zhè zuò qiáo de jiàn zhù gōng chéng。
He directed the building of the new bridge.

他买了一床厚被子过冬。
tā mǎi le yī chuáng hòu bèi zi guò dōng。
He bought a heavy quilt for the winter.

他从人群中挤过去。
tā zòng rén qún zhòng jǐ guò qu。
He forced his way through the crowd.

他从箱子里拿出一本书。
tā zòng xiāng zǐ lǐ ná chū yī běn shū。
He took out a book from the case.

他以晓之以礼的态度劝说她。
tā yǐ xiǎo zhī yǐ lǐ de tài du quàn shuō tā。
He talked to her with persuasive manner.

他们一家常在树林里野餐。
tā men yī jiā cháng zài shù lín lǐ yě cān。
Their family often picnics in the woods.

他们估计参观者人数为1000万。
tā men gū jì cān guān zhě rén shù wèī000 wàn。
They estimated the number of visitors at 10 million.

他们使用紫外线灯杀死害虫。
tā men shǐ yòng zǐ wài xiàn dēng shā sǐ hài chóng。
They use ultraviolet lamp to kill pests.

他们俩都想得到这职位。
tā men liǎng dōu xiǎng dé dào zhè zhí wèi。
They both try for the position.

他们又提高了汽油的价格。
tā men yòu tí gāo le qì yóu de jià gé。
They have increased the price of petrol again.

他们在沙漠中迷路而渴死了.
tā men zài shā mò zhòng mí lù ér kě sǐ le.
They lost their way in the desert and died of thirst.

他们在议会中互相吹捧。
tā men zài yì huì zhòng hù xiāng chuī pěng。
They clawed each other in Parliament.

他们拿起武器保卫祖国。
tā men ná qǐ wǔ qì bǎo wèi zǔ guó。
They took up arms in defence of their country.

他们热烈地欢迎主席。
tā men rè liè de huān yíng zhǔ xí。
They gave the chairman a tumultuous welcome.

他们用卡车运煤。
tā men yòng kǎ chē yùn méi。
They use a lorry to carry coals.

他们站在那，互相怒视着对方。
tā men zhàn zài nà， hù xiāng nù shì zhuó duì fāng。
They stood there, glaring at each other.

他们约定不久见面。
tā men yuē dìng bù jiǔ jiàn miàn。
They made a date to meet soon.

他们要求立即付款。
tā men yāo qiú lì jí fù kuǎn。
They demand prompt payment.

他们计划组织一次科学考察。
tā men jì huà zǔ zhī yī cì kē xué kǎo chá。
They planned to organize a scientific expedition.

他似乎不愿离去。
tā sì hu bù yuàn lí qù。
He seemed somewhat loath to depart.

他似乎把正号误作负号了。
tā sì hu bǎ zhèng hào wù zuò fù hào le。
He seems to have mistaken a plus for a minus.

他决定到我们的岛上居住。
tā jué dìng dào wǒ men de dǎo shàng jū zhù。
He decided to dwell on our island.

他划船渡过湖面。
tā huà chuán dù guò hú miàn。
He rowed the boat across the lake.

他刚刚到达就不得不又离开。
tā gāng gang dào dá jiù bù dé bù yòu lí kāi。
Scarcely had he arrived when he had to leave again.

他刮胡须时割破了脸.
tā guā hú xū shí gē pò le liǎn.
He cut himself/his face shaving.

他去年入党了。
tā qù nián rù dǎng le。
He was admitted to the Party last year.

他向我求婚，但我拒绝了。
tā xiàng wǒ qiú hūn， dàn wǒ jù jué le。
He asked me to marry him but I refused.

他向湖里扔了一块石头。
tā xiàng hú lǐ rēng le yī kuài shí tou。
He threw a stone into the lake.

他在战争中的英勇人所共见。
tā zài zhàn zhēng zhòng dì yīng yǒng rén suǒ gòng xiàn。
His valour in the war was seen by everybody.

他在抬沉重的家具时扭伤了腰。
tā zài tái chén zhòng de jiā jù shí niǔ shāng le yāo。
He did his back in lifting heavy furniture.

他在最适当的时候到达。
tā zài zuì shì dàng de shí hou dào dá。
He arrived at the most opportune moment.

他坐在沙发上, 点燃了一只香烟。
tā zuò zài shā fā shàng,  diǎn rán le yī zhǐ xiāng yān。
He had his seat in the sofa and lit a cigar.

他太小气，不肯请我们吃饭。
tā tài xiǎo qì， bù kěn qǐng wǒ men chī fàn。
He's too mean to buy us a meal.

他学习日语的兴趣逐渐消失了。
tā xué xí rì yǔ de xìng qu zhú jiàn xiāo shī le。
His interest in learning Japanese has petered out.

他对自己的缺点十分清楚。
tā duì zì jǐ de quē diǎn shí fēn qīng chu。
He was very conscious of his shortcomings.

他对著镜子看领带是否系正.
tā duì著 jìng zi kàn lǐng dài shì fǒu xì zhèng.
He looked in the glass to check that his tie was straight.

他尽管有病，还是可以上课。
tā jǐn guǎn yǒu bìng， hái shì kě yǐ shàng kè。
He is not so sick but he can attend a class.

他常去那个教堂做礼拜。
tā cháng qù nèi gè jiào táng zuò lǐ bài。
He is a regular worshiper at that church.

他心地善良。
tā xīn de shàn liáng。
He has a kind heart.

他想在餐具室里找到一些酒。
tā xiǎng zài cān jù shì lǐ zhǎo dào yī xiē jiǔ。
He wanted to find some wine in the pantry.

他把一盒食品从汽车上拿进来。
tā bǎ yī hé shí pǐn zòng qì chē shàng ná jìn lái。
He brought the box of groceries in from the car.

他把硬币倒过来，仔细检查。
tā bǎ yìng bì dào guò lai， zǐ xì jiǎn chá。
He reversed the coin and examined it carefully.

他把网球打过了网。
tā bǎ wǎng qiú dǎ guò le wǎng。
He hit the tennis ball over the net.

他把醋洒在鱼和土豆片上。
tā bǎ cù sǎ zài yú huò tǔ dòu piàn shàng。
He sprinkled vinegar on his fish and chips.

他掌握会议可真有一套.
tā zhǎng wò huì yì kě zhēn yǒu yī tào.
His handling of the meeting was quite a virtuoso performance.

他推我，我跌了下来。
tā tuī wǒ， wǒ diē le xia lai。
He pushed me and I fell over.

他推着手推车沿路走过。
tā tuī zhū shǒu tuī jū yàn lù zǒu guò。
He trundled a wheelbarrow down the path.

他无礼至极，竟然叫我傻瓜。
tā wú lǐ zhì jí， jìng rán jiào wǒ shǎ guā。
He was impudent enough to call me a fool.

他既不会读也不会写。
tā jì bù huì dú yě bù kuài xiě。
He can neither read nor write.

他时常提出一些奇怪的问题。
tā shí cháng tí chū yī xiē qí guài de wèn tí。
He raises some strange questions now and again.

他昨天到达的。
tā zuó tiān dào dá de。
He arrived yesterday.

他是个有个性的人。
tā shì gè yǒu gè xìng de rén。
He is a man of individuality.

他是为历史学教授。
tā shì wèi lì shǐ xué jiào shòu。
He is a professor of history.

他是第一个到达那里的。
tā shì dì yī gè dào dá nà li de。
He was the first to be there.

他有一些很奇怪的政治信念。
tā yǒu yī xiē hěn qí guài de zhèng zhì xìn niàn。
He has some pretty strange political ideas.

他有一双套鞋。
tā yǒu yī shuāng tào xié。
He has a pair of overshoes.

他正沿海边走去。
tā zhèng yán hǎi biān zǒu qù。
He is walking down the seaside.

他每次度假都会带他的狗去。
tā měi cì dù jià dū huì dài tā de gǒu qù。
He never goes on a vacation but he takes his pet dog.

他没多少文化修养。
tā mò duō shao wén huà xiū yǎng。
He is a man of little culture.

他没意识到自己犯了错误。
tā mò yì shí dào zì jǐ fàn le cuò wù。
He was unconscious of his mistake.

他渴望回到故乡。
tā kě wàng huí dào gù xiàng。
He yearned to return to his native land.

他用一则有趣的笑话结束了演讲。
tā yòng yī zé yǒu qù de xiào huà jié shù le yǎn jiǎng。
He closed his speech with a funny joke.

他用一张小的王牌吃了我的A牌。
tā yòng yī zhāng xiǎo de wáng pái jí le wǒ deA pái。
He took my ace with a low trump.

他的专业是比较文学。
tā de zhuān yè shì bǐ jiào wén xué。
He majored in comparative literature.

他的书上个月出版了。
tā de shū shàng gè yuè chū bǎn le。
His book came out last month.

他的人生观与你的不同。
tā de rén shēng guàn yù nǐ de bù tóng。
His view of life is different from yours.

他的叔叔教他法语。
tā de shū shu jiào tā fǎ yǔ。
His uncle instructed him in French.

他的头一阵阵地痛。
tā de tou yī zhèn zhèn dì tòng。
His head throbbed with pain.

他的头发已剪短了。
tā de tóu fa yǐ jiǎn duǎn le。
His hair has been cut short.

他的左胳膊在一次事故中受伤了。
tā de zuǒ gē bo zài yī cì shì gù zhòng shòu shāng le。
His left arm was hurt in an accident.

他的态度带有几分傲慢。
tā de tài du dài yǒu jǐ fèn ào màn。
His manner partakes of insolence.

他的梦想实现了。
tā de mèng xiǎng shí xiàn le。
His dream came true.

他的火车头模型缺了一个零件.
tā de huǒ chē tóu mó xíng quē le yī gè líng jiàn.
He lost one of the pieces of his model engine.

他的眼光转向了电话机。
tā de yǎn guāng zhuǎn xiàng le diàn huà jī。
His eyes shifted to the telephone.

他的行为招致尖锐的批评。
tā de xíng wéi zhāo zhì jiān ruì de pī píng。
His behavior called forth sharp criticism.

他的言行就好像没有常识似的。
tā de yán xìng jiù hǎo xiàng méi yǒu cháng shí sì de。
He behaves as if he had no common sense.

他的计划迅速变为现实。
tā de jì huà xùn sù biàn wèi xiàn shí。
His plans were transformed overnight into reality.

他的讲话赢得了听众的掌声。
tā de jiǎng huà yíng dé le tīng zhòng de zhǎng shēng。
His speech won the applause of the audience.

他的诗集去年发表了。
tā de shī jí qù nián fā biǎo le。
His poetry was published last year.

他稍微会一点儿日语.
tā shāo wēi kuài yī diǎnr rì yǔ.
He has some little acquaintance with the Japanese language.

他穿着一套黑西装。
tā chuān zhuó yī tào hēi xī zhuāng。
He is wearing a black suit.

他站在门口, 堵住通向大厅的路.
tā zhàn zài mén kǒu,  dǔ zhù tōng xiàng dà tīng de lù.
He stood framed in the doorway to the hall.

他笨手笨脚的漏接了球。
tā bèn shǒu bèn jué de lòu jiē le qiú。
He fumbled the ball and then dropped it.

他经常按他妻子的吩咐去做。
tā jīng cháng àn tā qī zi de fēn fù qù zuò。
He often does his wife's bidding.

他花了半个小时做完这项工作。
tā huā le bàn gè xiǎo shí zuò wán zhè xiàng gōng zuò。
It took him half an hour to finish the work.

他被定为一号种子选手。
tā bèi dìng wèi yī hào zhǒng zi xuǎn shǒu。
He was seeded number 1.

他警告我晚上不要到那去。
tā jǐng gào wǒ wǎn shang bù yào dào nà qù。
He warned me against going there at night.

他计划去南美。
tā jì huà qù Nán měi。
He purposed to visit South America.

他该保持安静是有必要的。
tā gāi bǎo chí ān jìng shì yǒu bì yào de。
It is important that he be quiet.

他躺在沙发上看电视.
tā tǎng zài shā fā shàng kàn diàn shì.
He was lying on the sofa watching TV.

他轻而易举地完成了这项工作。
tā qīng ér yì jǔ de wán chéng le zhè xiàng gōng zuò。
He finished the work without any difficulty.

他问马车夫以前是否去过那里。
tā wèn mǎ chē fū yǐ qián shì fǒu qù guò nà li。
He asked the carter if he had been there before.

他骗我把自行车借给了他。
tā piàn wǒ bǎ zì xíng chē jiè jǐ le tā。
He beguiled me into lending him my bicycle.

任何值得做的事就值得做好。
rèn hé zhí de zuò de shì jiù zhí de zuò hào。
Whatever is worth doing at all is worth doing well.

会议每年举行一次。
huì yì měi nián jǔ xíng yī cì。
The meeting is held yearly.

体育运动有益健康。
tǐ yù yùn dòng yǒu yì jiàn kāng。
Athletic sports are good to the health.

你们的运动不断取得进展.
nǐ men de yùn dòng bù duàn qǔ dé jìn zhǎn.
Your campaign is gaining ground.

你刚才讲的话彻底离题了。
nǐ gāng cái jiǎng de huà chè dǐ lí tí le。
What you just said is completely off the track.

你看上去心虚。
nǐ kàn shàng qù xīn xū。
You look guilty.

你知道我多么讨厌打字和速记。
nǐ zhī dào wǒ duō me tǎo yàn dǎ zì huò sù jì。
You know how I loathe typing and shorthand.

你说话太不礼貌了，我已受够了。
nǐ shuō huà tài bù lǐ mào le， wǒ yǐ shòu gòu le。
I've had enough of your impertinent words.

信封内装有几份附件。
xìn fēng nèi zhuāng yǒu jǐ fèn fù jiàn。
There are several enclosures in the envelope.

修筑一条铁路要花费许多劳动力。
xiū zhù yī tiáo tiě lù yào huā fèi xǔ duō láo dòng lì。
It takes a lot of labor to build a railway.

俱乐部会馆提供这样方便的建筑物
jù yuè bù kuài guǎn tí gōng zhè yàng fāng biàn de jiàn zhù wù
A building housing such facilities.

候任总统将在下周正式就任。
hòu rèn zǒng tǒng jiàng zài xià zhōu zhèng shì jiù rèn。
The President elect will be installed next week.

偷吃而不被人发现很有趣。
tōu jí ér bù bèi rén fā xiàn hěn yǒu qù。
It is fun eating by stealth without being found.

儿童的鞋并不便宜--反而更贵.
ér tóng de xié bìng bù pián yi-- fǎn ér gèng guì.
Children's shoes aren't cheap quite the reverse.

先读课文，然后解释生词。
xiān dú kè wén， rán hòu jiě shì shēng cí。
Read the text first and then explain the new words.

再呆10个星期，一共3个月。
zài dāī0 gè xīng qī， yí gò3ng gè yuè。
Another ten weeks three months altogether.

再见，旅途愉快。
zài jiàn， lu:3 tú yú kuài。
Good-bye, and have a nice journey.

农民们正在收割大麦。
nóng mín men zhèng zài shōu gē dà mài。
The peasants are reaping a field of barley.

冬天是大多数旅馆的淡季。
dōng tiān shì dà duō shù lu:3 guǎn de dàn jì。
Winter is the slack season at most hotels.

出国前我必须进行体格检查。
chū guó qián wǒ bì xū jìn xíng tǐ gé jiǎn chá。
I have to have a medical examination before going abroad.

出门之前把窗户关严。
chū mén zhī qián bǎ chuāng hu guān yán。
Make the windows secure before leaving the house.

别忘了带上你的钓具。
biè wàng le dài shàng nǐ de diào jù。
Don't forget to bring your fishing tackle.

别忘了给服务员小费.
biè wàng le jǐ fú wù yuán xiǎo fèi.
Please remember (ie Don't forget to tip) the waiter.

别担心，我会支持你的。
biè dān xīn， wǒ kuài zhī chí nǐ de。
Do not fear; I will support you.

别着急，安心养病。
biè zháo jí， ān xīn yǎng bìng。
Just take care of yourself and don't worry.

别胡闹了，过来给我帮个忙。
biè hú nào le， guò lai jǐ wǒ bāng gè máng。
Stop fucking around and come and give me a hand.

别让她在外边雨中等著.
biè ràng tā zài wài biān yǔ zhōng děng著.
Don't leave her waiting outside in the rain.

别让我失望。

从他领导后，一个又一个革新项目出现了。

从这个角度来看, 画中的女子面带微笑.

他们从远处赶来参观这个展览会。

他们爱举行戏称之为文学晚会的活动.
tā men ài jǔ xíng xì chèng zhī wèi wén xué wǎn huì de huó dòng.
They're fond of holding what are laughingly known as literary soirees.

他们的研究沿着正确的方针进行。

他们的观点同我们看问题的方法格格不入。

他们的足球队在昨天的比赛中表现突出。

Their football team performed very well in the match yesterday.

他们看着电视里的快步舞并且试图模仿。

他们看见了灯塔发出一闪一灭的光。

他们试图预测这场足球比赛的结果。

他伸出手去，保护他的孩子免受伤害。

他体重减了很多, 比以前轻了三公斤.

他做的事完全合法, 警方不能碰他.

他冒着自己的生命危险救了我的命。

他向我走来，微笑著伸出手来和我握手。

他听到身后有响声，便转过身来。

他回过身来, 帮助那位扭了脚的朋友。

他在我背上拍了一下，请我去喝酒。
tā zài wǒ bèi shàng pāi le yī xià， qǐng wǒ qù hē jiǔ。

他在物理学方面已经取得了巨大成就。
tā zài wù lǐ xué fāng miàn yǐ jīng qǔ dé le jù dà chéng jiù。

他在那个伸出到街上的阳台上种了些花。

他在面对危险的时候表现出非凡的勇气。

He showed remarkable courage when he faced the danger.

他对他的选民表现出很有感染力的热情。

他对友谊有一种非常独特的见解。
tā duì yǒu yì yǒu yī zhòng fēi cháng dú tè de jiàn jiě。

他对学校课外活动一点也不积极。
tā duì xué xiào kè wài huó dòng yī diǎn yě bù jī jí。
He doesn't take an active part in many school activities.

他对环境的新奇感不久就淡薄了。
tā duì huán jìng de xīn qí gǎn bù jiǔ jiù dàn bó le。
The novelty of his surroundings soon wore off.

他已学了足够的德语来进行会话。
tā yǐ xué le zú gòu de dé yǔ lái jìn xíng huì huà。
He had learned enough German to carry on a conversation.

他已经通过了大学的入学考试。
tā yǐ jīng tōng guò le dà xué de rù xué kǎo shì。
He had passed the entrance examination of the college.

他带着心满意足的微笑告诉了我们。
tā dài zhuó xīn mǎn yì zú de wēi xiào gào su le wǒ men。
He told us with a smile of contentment.

他摇摇头，因为他的想法与此不同。
tā yáo yáo tou， yīn wèi tā de xiǎng fǎ yù cǐ bù tóng。
He shook his head, for he thought differently.

他收拾行李，让我们等了好半天。
tā shōu shi xíng li， ràng wǒ men děng le hào bàn tiān。
He kept us waiting for ages while he packed his luggage.

他收集的邮票是我的三倍还不止。
tā shōu jí de yóu piào shì wǒ de sān bèi huán bù zhǐ。
He has collected more than three times as many stamps as I (have).

他是那些天文学家中最优秀的一个。
tā shì nà xiē tiān wén xué jiā zhòng zuì yōu xiù de yī gè。
He is the best one of those astronomers.

他毕业于一所知名的外语学院。
tā bì yè yú yī suǒ zhī míng de wài yǔ xué yuàn。
He graduated from a famous foreign language institute.

他爸爸坚持他们应该搬到乡下。
tā bà ba jiān chí tā men yīng gāi bān dào xiāng xià。

wǒ men kě yǐ tōng guò shāo shí huī shí lái dé dào shí huī。
We may burn limestone to obtain lime.

我们复制了计算机磁盘以防意外。
wǒ men fù zhì le jì suàn jī cí pán yǐ fáng yì wài。
We make copies of our computer disks as a safeguard against accidents.

我们大家都得参加跑步训练, 无人例外.
wǒ men dà jiā dōu de cān jiā pǎo bù xùn liàn,  wú rén lì wài.
We all had to take part in the training run, with nobody excepted.

我们应充分利用丰富的人力资源。
wǒ men yìng chōng fèn lì yòng fēng fù de rén lì zī yuán。
We shall take full advantage of our rich source of human beings.

我们应该使用无烟煤以防止空气污染。
wǒ men yīng gāi shǐ yòng wú yān méi yǐ fáng zhǐ kōng qì wū rǎn。
We should use anthracite to avoid air pollution.

我们应该多吃一些富含纤维素的绿色蔬菜。
wǒ men yīng gāi duō jí yī xiē fù hán xiān wéi sù de lu:4 sè shū cài。
We should eat more green vegetables rich in cellulose.

我们很难观察月亮的另一边。
wǒ men hěn nàn guān chá yuè liàng de lìng yī biān。
The far side of the moon is difficult for us to observe.

我们得设计出三年级的新课程.
wǒ men de shè jì chū sān nián jí de xīn kè chéng.
We shall have to design a new curriculum for the third year.

我们既不将打篮球也不将打排球。
wǒ men jì bù jiàng dǎ lán qiú yě bù jiàng dǎ pái qiú。
We are going to play neither basketball nor volleyball.

我们昨天碰到的那个老工人是李师傅。
wǒ men zuó tiān pèng dào de nèi gè lǎo gōng rén shì lǐ shī fu。
The old worker whom we met yesterday is Master Li.

我们用他给我们带来的面粉做了一些面包。
wǒ men yòng tā jǐ wǒ men dài lái de miàn fěn zuò le yī xiē miàn bāo。
We made some bread with the flour he bought for us.

我们用电脑查找所有用连字符连接的词。
wǒ men yòng diàn nǎo chá zhǎo suǒ yǒu yòng lián zì fú lián jiē de cí。
We did a computer search for all the hyphenated words.

我们的假日过得好无聊，每天都下雨。
wǒ men de jià rì guò de hào wú liáo， měi tiān dōu xià yǔ。
We had a mouldy holiday - it rained every day.

我们的房子离村中两家酒馆距离相等.
wǒ men de fáng zi lí cūn zhòng liǎng jiā jiǔ guǎn jù lí xiāng děng.
Our house is equidistant from the two pubs in the village.

我们的文艺必须为大众所喜闻乐见。
wǒ men de wén yì bì xū wèi dà zhòng suǒ xǐ wén yuè xiàn。
Our literature and art ought to cater to popular taste.

我们跟服务员争执那顿饭的价钱.
wǒ men gēn fú wù yuán zhēng zhí nà dùn fàn de jià qian.
We argued with the waiter about the price of the meal.

我们除了同意他们之外，没有别的选择。
wǒ men chú le tóng yì tā men zhī wài， méi yǒu bié de xuǎn zé。
We have no other choice than to agree with them.

我们需要一个更为灵活的外交政策。
wǒ men xū yào yī gè gèng wèi líng huó de wài jiāo zhèng cè。
We need a foreign policy that is more flexible.

我们需要几个男子作心理学实验对象.
wǒ men xū yào jǐ ge nán zǐ zuò xīn lǐ xué shí yàn duì xiàng.
We need some male subjects for a psychology experiment.

我会陪在你身边，就象我答应你的那样。
wǒ kuài péi zài nǐ shēn biān， jiù xiàng wǒ dā ying nǐ de nà yàng。
I will be at your side, as I promised you.

我儿子六岁的时候开始学习乘法。
wǒ ér zi liù suì de shí hou kāi shǐ xué xí chéng fǎ。
My son began to study multiplication when he was six.

我养了一只猫和一只狗，但它们老是打架。
wǒ yǎng le yī zhǐ māo huò yī zhǐ gǒu， dàn tā men lǎo shi dǎ jià。
I have a dog and a cat, but they fight all the time.

我出生在河北省的一个小村庄。
wǒ chū shēng zài hé běi shěng de yī gè xiǎo cūn zhuāng。
I was born in a small village in Hebei Province.

我刚好及时到会，才算没受责备。
wǒ gāng hǎo jí shí dào kuài， cái suàn mò shòu zé bèi。
I saved my bacon by arriving just in time for the meeting.

我只好解释原因来满足他的好奇心。
wǒ zhǐ hǎo jiě shì yuán yīn lái mǎn zú tā de hào qí xīn。
I had to explain the reasons to satisfy his curiosity.

我喜欢滑雪, 同时也知道这非常危险。
wǒ xǐ huan huá xuě,  tóng shí yě zhī dào zhè fēi cháng wēi xiǎn。
I like skiing and in the meantime, I know it is very dangerous.

我因有约在先，所以未能参加这个会。
wǒ yīn yǒu yuē zài xiān， suǒ yǐ wèi néng cān jiā zhè gè kuài。
I was unable to attend the meeting because of a prior engagement.

我在七点钟的新闻报道中听到了这则消息。
wǒ zài qī diǎn zhōng de xīn wén bào dào zhòng tīng dào le zhè zé xiāo xi。
I heard it on the 7 o'clock news.

我在人群中寻找她，但看不到。
wǒ zài rén qún zhòng xún zhǎo tā， dàn kàn bù dào。
I looked for her in the crowd but couldn't see her.

我已经在这个旅馆里预订了一个房间。
wǒ yǐ jīng zài zhè gè lu:3 guǎn lǐ yù dìng le yī gè fáng jiān。
I have engaged a room at this hotel.

我希望他别再招待他的朋友了。
wǒ xī wàng tā biè zài zhāo dài tā de péng you le。
I wish he would desist from entertaining his friends.

我开始作画，仅仅是最近的事情。
wǒ kāi shǐ zuò huà， jǐn jǐn shì zuì jìn de shì qing。
It is only recently that I started painting.

我开始做这项工作时, 遇到许多困难.
wǒ kāi shǐ zuò zhè xiàng gōng zuò shí,  yù dào xǔ duō kùn nan.
I encountered many difficulties when I first started this job.

我很忙，所以不得不中断每周的访问。
wǒ hěn máng， suǒ yǐ bù dé bù zhōng duàn měi zhōu de fǎng wèn。
I'm so busy that I have to discontinue weekly visits.

我得把电话号码记下来，以免待会儿忘记。
wǒ de bǎ diàn huà hào mǎ jì xia lai， yǐ miǎn dài kuài er wàng jì。
I'll just jot down their phone number before I forget it.

我总觉得他讨厌我，但我不知道为什么。
wǒ zǒng jué de tā tǎo yàn wǒ， dàn wǒ bù zhī dào wèi shén me。
I always feel he has a grudge against me, although I don't know why.

我把一个长方形的盒子放在桌子上。
wǒ bǎ yī gè zhǎng fāng xíng de hé zi fàng zài zhuō zi shàng。
I put a rectangular box on the table.

我拿起了那把刀，把它扔到了窗外。
wǒ ná qǐ le nà bǎ dāo， bǎ tā rēng dào le chuāng wài。
I picked up the knife and threw it out of the window.

我有一件红色的有羊毛衬里的运动服。
wǒ yǒu yī jiàn hóng sè de yǒu yáng máo chèn lǐ de yùn dòng fú。
I have a red tracksuit with fleecy lining.

我每天至少要把厨房地板擦洗一次。
wǒ měi tiān zhì shǎo yào bǎ chú fáng dì bǎn cā xǐ yī cì。
I have to mop the kitchen floor at least once a day.

我清楚地告诉他，我拒绝了他的建议。
wǒ qīng chu de gào su tā， wǒ jù jué le tā de jiàn yì。
I made it clear to him that I rejected his proposal.

我用一个纸夹把那几页纸夹在一起。
wǒ yòng yī gè zhǐ jiā bǎ nà jǐ yè zhǐ jiā zài yī qǐ。
I fastened the pages together with a paperclip.

我的起居室的墙上挂着一块壁毯。
wǒ de qǐ jū shì de qiáng shàng guà zhuó yī kuài bì tǎn。
The wall of my living room was hung with a tapestry.

我等她回来时，心里越来越不安。
wǒ děng tā huí lai shí， xīn lǐ yuè lái yuè bù ān。
I waited with growing uneasiness for her to return.

我答应一定完好无损地还你的自行车。
wǒ dā ying yī dìng wán hǎo wú sǔn de huán nǐ de zì xíng chē。
I promise to return your bicycle on good condition.

我舒适地靠在大沙发上，开始看小说。
wǒ shū shì de kào zài dà shā fā shàng， kāi shǐ kàn xiǎo shuō。
I nestled down on the big sofa and began to read novels.

我觉得我没有勇气告诉他这个坏消息。
wǒ jué de wǒ méi yǒu yǒng qì gào su tā zhè gè huài xiāo xi。
I don't think I have the courage to tell him the bad news.

我认为秋天是一年中最美的季节。
wǒ rèn wéi qiū tiān shì yī nián zhòng zuì měi de jì jié。
I think autumn is the most beautiful season in a year.

我认为这些有趣的旧习俗应该保存下去。
wǒ rèn wéi zhè xie yǒu qù de jiù xí sú yīng gāi bǎo cún xià qu。
I think these interesting old customs should be preserved.

我还不会游泳，但我用胳膊划了几下。
wǒ huán bù huì yóu yǒng， dàn wǒ yòng gē bo huà le jǐ xià。
I can't swim yet, but I've made a few strokes with my arms.

我连移动双脚的力气都几乎没有了。
wǒ lián yí dòng shuāng jué de lì qi dōu jī hū méi yǒu le。
I have hardly enough strength left to move my feet.

我队今年赛季赢五场而未输过.
wǒ duì jīn nián sài jì yíng wǔ chǎng ér wèi shū guò.
Our team has had five wins and no losses this season.

战争迫使我们不得不违背旧习俗。
zhàn zhēng pò shǐ wǒ men bù dé bù wéi bèi jiù xí sú。
The war forced us to depart from the old customs.

把你的名字填写在每页上端的括号内。
bǎ nǐ de míng zi tián xiě zài měi yè shàng duān de kuò hào nèi。
Put your name in brackets at the top of each page.

把被单好好煮一煮，好让它们白一些。
bǎ bèi shàn hǎo hǎo zhǔ yī zhǔ， hào ràng tā men bái yī xiē。
Give the sheets a good boil to get them white.

把这条句子的各个成份加以分析。
bǎ zhè tiáo jù zi de gè ge chéng fèn jiā yǐ fēn xī。

报纸上的这篇文章为他的演讲提供了启发。
bào zhǐ shàng de zhè piān wén zhāng wèi tā de yǎn jiǎng tí gōng le qǐ fā。
The newspaper article provided him with fuel for his speech.

担任主席的人有责任安排会议。
dān rèn zhǔ xí de rén yǒu zé rèn ān pái huì yì。
The holder of the office of chairman is responsible for arranging meetings.

拥有汽车的人数一直在逐渐上升。
yōng yǒu qì chē de rén shù yī zhí zài zhú jiàn shàng shēng。
There has been a gradual increase in the number of people owning cars.

政府对工会表现得越来越不耐烦。
zhèng fǔ duì gōng huì biǎo xiàn de yuè lái yuè bù nài fán。
The governments showed growing impatience at the unions.

政府还没有找出对付失业的有效措施。
zhèng fǔ huán méi yǒu zhǎo chū duì fu shī yè de yǒu xiào cuò shī。
The government hasn't worked out the effectual measures to combat unemployment.

教会应当就基本道德问题多做出些榜样.

The Church should give more of a lead on basic moral issues.

教师在学习中的关键作用是不该忽视的。
jiào shī zài xué xí zhòng dì guān jiàn zuò yòng shì bù gāi hū shì de。
The key role of the teacher in the learning process should not be neglected.

新制度已对生产力造成了灾难性的影响。
xīn zhì dù yǐ duì shēng chǎn lì zào chéng le zāi nàn xìng de yǐng xiǎng。
The new system has had a disastrous effect on productivity.

新学期开学前，我一直无所事事。
xīn xué qī kāi xué qián， wǒ yī zhí wú suǒ shì shì。
I'm just kicking my heels until the beginning of the new term.

早晨很冷，他穿上了一件厚毛衣。
zǎo chén hěn lěng， tā chuān shàng le yī jiàn hòu máo yī。
He put on a thick sweater since it was cold in the morning.

春天的时候，踩在松软的地面上非常舒服。

It's very comfortable to step on the soft ground in the spring.

最后他终于成功地解决了这个问题。
zuì hòu tā zhōng yú chéng gōng de jiě jué le zhè gè wèn tí。
At last he successfully solved the problem.

最小的儿童上一年级, 最大的上六年级.

The youngest children are in the first form, the oldest in the sixth form.

有关环境的会议将在下周一举行。
yǒu guān huán jìng de huì yì jiàng zài xià zhōu yī jǔ xíng。
The convocation about environment will be held on next Monday.

有天晚上学校放映了一部西部片。
yǒu tiān wǎn shang xué xiào fàng yìng le yī bù xī bù piàn。

有约在先，我恐怕不能与你共进晚餐。
yǒu yuē zài xiān， wǒ kǒng pà bù néng yù nǐ gòng jìn wǎn cān。
I fear that a prior engagement will prohibit me from joining you in dinner.

本世纪我们已经经历了两次世界大战。
běn shì jì wǒ men yǐ jīng jīng lì le liǎng cì shì jiè dà zhàn。
We have had two world wars in this century.

běn bān nán shēng de píng jūn nián líng shì shí wǔ suì。

机场当局已答应重新检查他们的安全措施。

法庭上原告和被告双方都有各自的律师。

The French teacher dictates to the class every other week.

火警警报响时全体人员应到楼外集合.

父亲给我买了一只小狗作为生日礼物。

狮子一走近，小动物们都跑开了。

生命可以被比作一次不知目的地的旅行。
shēng mìng kě yǐ bèi bì zuò yī cì bù zhī mù dì dì de lu:3 xíng。

生日晚会之后, 房间里一片混乱。

电影导演测试了一下那位新演员的演技。

目前似乎好的年轻选手太少了。

等到我得知这项决定时，已经太迟了。

I wasn't informed of the decision until too late.

jiǎn dān pǔ sù de yī fu shì hé zài xué xiào lǐ chuān。

管理部门采取了一切合理的安全措施。

The management took all reasonable safety precautions.

经济知识对于理解这个问题是至关重要的。

群众高声喊叫把演讲人的声音压了下去。

zòng jǐ ge lì zi zhòng jǐn jǐ nǐ jǔ chū yī lì....

tā zhuān xīn dú bào,  lián mén líng yě mò tīng jiàn。

他为了养家不得不去拼命工作。
tā wèi le yǎng jiā bù dé bù qù pīn mìng gōng zuò。

tā yǐ yī zhāng qiàn tiáo dài tì xiàn jīn fù jǐ wǒ men。

tā men réng zài wèi jué sài shī bài ér shāng xīn.

他们以唱歌来减轻等候的厌烦.

tā men gū jì cān guān zhě rén shù wèī000 wàn。

tā men shǐ yòng zǐ wài xiàn dēng shā sǐ hài chóng。

他们决定明天去田野里打野兔。
tā men jué dìng míng tiān qù tián yě lǐ dǎ yě tù。

他们只用天然颜料染毛织品。
tā men zhǐ yòng tiān rán yán liào rǎn máo zhī pǐn。

tā men duì guān fāng de zhèng cè biǎo shì chū yì yì。

他们很冷淡地接待了这位首相.
tā men hěn lěng dàn de jiē dài le zhè wèi shǒu xiàng.

他们拣拾木柴以补充煤的不足.
tā men jiǎn shí mù chái yǐ bǔ chōng méi de bù zú.

他们断言这个女孩子读了不少书。
tā men duàn yán zhè gè nu:3 hái zi dú le bù shǎo shū。

他们用冲床在金属板上打孔。
tā men yòng chòng chuáng zài jīn shǔ bǎn shàng dǎ kǒng。

他们的研究沿着正确的方针进行。
tā men de yán jiū yán zhe zhèng què de fāng zhēn jìn xíng。

他们站在那，互相怒视着对方。
tā men zhàn zài nà， hù xiāng nù shì zhuó duì fāng。

rén men cháng shuō nu:3 rén bì nán rén gèng fù yú gǎn qíng。

rén men yìng jīng cháng xǐ zǎo yǐ bǎo zhèng gè rén wèi shēng。

Seen from this angle the woman in the picture is smiling.

他上学时有时到羽毛球俱乐部去。
tā shàng xué shí yǒu shí dào yǔ máo qiú jù yuè bù qù。

他下决心每天要读一小时有益读物。

他不会放弃任何机会以获得一份好工作。

他不喜欢对他自己的所作所为作出解释。

他似乎没有意识到形势的严重性。

加入的液体太多，混合液的浓度就不够。
jiā rù de yè tǐ tài duō， hùn hé yè de nóng dù jiù bù gòu。
If you add too much liquid the mixture will not be thick enough.

劳资双方之间存在大量矛盾.
láo zī shuāng fāng zhī jiān cún zài dà liàng máo dùn.
There is a great deal of friction between the management and the work force.

劳资双方仍在商谈制订和解方案.
láo zī shuāng fāng réng zài shāng tán zhì dìng hé jiě fāng àn.
Managers and workers are still working out a peace formula.

医术，医业，医学有关医学的技术和专业
yī zhú， yī yè， yī xué yǒu guān yī xué de jì shù huò zhuān yè
The art or profession of medicine.

印刷字体太小，我不带眼镜就看不清。
yìn shuà zì tǐ tài xiǎo， wǒ bù dài yǎn jìng jiù kàn bù qīng。
The print is too small for me to read without glasses.

印度向许多国家出口茶叶和棉花.
Yìn dù xiàng xǔ duō guó jiā chū kǒu chá yè huò mián hua.
India exports tea and cotton to many different countries.

参赛者中包括三名世界记录保持者。
shēn sài zhě zhòng bāo kuò sān míng shì jiè jì lù bǎo chí zhě。
The field includes three world record holders.

双方军队在边境的冲突引发了战争。
shuāng fāng jūn duì zài biān jìng de chōng tū yǐn fā le zhàn zhēng。
A border clash between the two armies started the war.

发明了印刷术后文化教育才得以普及。
fā míng le yìn shuà zhú hòu wén huà jiào yù cái dé yǐ pǔ jí。
Mass literacy was only possible after the invention of printing.

只有一个人能做这项工作，那就是你。
zhǐ yǒu yī gè rén néng zuò zhè xiàng gōng zuò， nà jiù shì nǐ。
Only one person can do the job, namely you.

只有时间才能使人淡忘那些不快的记忆。
zhǐ yǒu shí jiān cái néng shǐ rén dàn wàng nà xiē bù kuài de jì yì。
Time alone will efface those unpleasant memories.

只有练习能帮你熟练地用眼作出判断。
zhǐ yǒu liàn xí néng bāng nǐ shú liàn de yòng yǎn zuò chū pàn duàn。
Only practice can help you to keep your eye in.

只知道一点点，不如完全不晓得。
zhǐ zhī dào yī diǎn diǎn， bù rú wán quán bù xiǎo de。
You might as well not know a thing at all as know it only a little.

只要我们紧密团结就能克服困难。
zhǐ yào wǒ men jǐn mì tuán jié jiù néng kè fú kùn nan。
We can surely overcome these difficulties as long as we are closely united.

只要把它完成了，你怎么做我并不计较。
zhǐ yào bǎ tā wán chéng le， nǐ zěn me zuò wǒ bìng bù jì jiào。
I'm not particular how you do it as long as it gets done.

吵闹的年青人都已从影院被逐出去了。
chǎo nào de nián qīng rén dōu yǐ zòng yǐng yuàn bèi zhú chū qù le。
The noisy youths were ejected from the cinema.

吸烟有害健康，这是大家公认的。
xī yān yǒu hài jiàn kāng， zhè shì dà jiā gōng rèn de。
It is generally accepted that smoking is harmful to our health.

咱们不要在现阶段著手处理具体问题。
zán men bù yào zài xiàn jiē duàn著 shǒu chǔ lǐ jù tǐ wèn tí。
Let's not enter into details at this stage.

咱们定好下次会议的时间和地点吧.
zán men dìng hào xià cì huì yì de shí jiān huò dì diǎn ba.
Let's arrange a time and place for our next meeting.

哎呀，我把毛活儿落在公共汽车上了。
āi yā， wǒ bǎ máo huór luò zài gōng gòng qì chē shàng le。
Oh dear, I've left my knitting on the bus!

商店趁一时缺货而提高价格从中获利。
shāng diàn chèn yī shí quē huò ér tí gāo jià gé cóng zhōng huò lì。
The shop is cashed in on temporary shortage by raising price.

因无人维持秩序, 教室里一片混乱.

With no one to keep order the situation in the classroom was chaotic.

图书管理员从书架上随便拿了一本书。
tú shū guǎn lǐ yuán zòng shū jià shàng suí biàn ná le yī běn shū。
The librarian took a book at random from the shelf.

在中世纪, 哲学与神学是不分的.
zài zhòng shì jì,  zhé xué yù shén xué shì bù fēn de.
In the Middle Ages, philosophy and theology were inextricable.

在中国，山区农民在梯田上种水稻。
zài Zhōng guó， shān qū nóng mín zài tī tián shàng zhòng shuǐ dào。
In China hill farmers grow rice on terraces.

在他到达车间之前，机器已经开动了。
zài tā dào dá chē jiān zhī qián， jī qì yǐ jīng kāi dòng le。
Before he gets to the workshop, the machine has been put in motion.

在会议之前，我们讨论了这个问题。
zài huì yì zhī qián， wǒ men tǎo lùn le zhè gè wèn tí。
Previous to the conference we had discussed the matter among ourselves.

在我国, 一般人家里没有集中供热设备.

People don't have central heating in their houses in my country.

在我看来，你跟他都没有达到标准。
zài wǒ kàn lai， nǐ gēn tā dōu méi yǒu dá dào biāo zhǔn。
In my opinion, neither you nor he has met the standard.

在我看来，我们会再次考试不及格的。
zài wǒ kàn lai， wǒ men kuài zài cì kǎo shì bù jí gé de。
It seems to me that we'll again fail in the exam.

在我祖父看来，我爸爸仍然是个小孩。
zài wǒ zǔ fù kàn lai， wǒ bà ba réng rán shì gè xiǎo hái。
It seems to my grandfather that my father is still a child.

在海上航行了三天，我们终于看见了大陆。
zài hǎi shàng háng xíng le sān tiān， wǒ men zhōng yú kàn jiàn le dà lù。
After three days at sea we sighted the land.

在等待开演的时候，演员们十分紧张
zài děng dài kāi yǎn de shí hou， yǎn yuán men shí fēn jǐn zhāng
The performers were edgy as they waited for the show to begin.

在考虑这一问题时，你应当抓住实质。
zài kǎo lu:4 zhè yī wèn tí shí， nǐ yīng dāng zhuā zhù shí zhì。
In considering this problem, you should grasp its essentials.

在资信方面, 这家商行还是很可靠的。
zài zī xìn fāng miàn,  zhè jiā shāng xìng hái shì hěn kě kào de。
In respect of financial standing, this firm is reliable.

在这一测验中你与专家较量一下技巧吧。
zài zhè yī cè yàn zhòng nǐ yù zhuān jiā jiào liàng yī xià jì qiǎo ba。
Match your skill against the experts in this quiz.

在这种时候应大力反对如此浪费金钱。

Such waste of money should be deprecated at a time like this.

The soldiers are ready at all times to smash the enemy's attacks.

大多数中国人认为他将从此不受欢迎。

dà jiā rèn wéi zuì hǎo zàn shí fàng qì zhè gè xiǎng fǎ。
It was thought best to drop the idea for the time being.

天黑了，我看不见这块石头上的碑文。

I can't read the inscription on this stone because it's getting dark.

女王在一所古老的大教堂里举行登基仪式。

The queen was enthroned in an ancient abbey.

她以自己的名义支持这一崇高的事业。
tā yǐ zì jǐ de míng yì zhī chí zhè yī chóng gāo de shì yè。
She has lent her name to the lofty cause.

她和他们打招呼时亲切地直呼其名.
tā huò tā men dǎ zhāo hu shí qīn qiè de zhí hū qí míng.
She greeted them by their first names in a familiar way.

她和她姐姐外貌相似，但性格不同。
tā huò tā jiě jie wài mào xiāng sì， dàn xìng gé bù tóng。
She resembles her sister in appearance but not in character.

她因那重要时刻渐近而越来越紧张.
tā yīn nà zhòng yào shí kè jiàn jìn ér yuè lái yuè jǐn zhāng.
As the great moment approached, she grew more and more nervous.

她在国内第一流指挥家中名列榜首.
tā zài guó nèi dì yī liú zhǐ huī jiā zhòng míng liè bǎng shǒu.
She ranks foremost among the country's leading conductors.

她在演讲时一直都在玩弄手帕。
tā zài yǎn jiǎng shí yī zhí dōu zài wán nòng shǒu pà。
She was playing with her handkerchief all the while during the speech.

她在这一切不幸中表现得很坚强。
tā zài zhè yī qiè bù xìng zhòng biǎo xiàn de hěn jiān qiáng。
She bore up well against all these misfortunes.

她大力鼓吹节约是解决危机的关键。
tā dà lì gǔ chuī jié yuē shì jiě jué wēi jī de guān jiàn。
She preached economy as the best means of solving the crisis.

她很独立，所以拒绝一切金钱上的资助。
tā hěn dú lì， suǒ yǐ jù jué yī qiè jīn qián shàng de zī zhù。
She is so independent that she refused all pecuniary aid.

她意识到在所采用的方法中可能出错.
tā yì shí dào zài suǒ cǎi yòng de fāng fǎ zhòng kě néng chū cuò.
She recognized the potential for error in the method being used.

她戴上墨镜以防强光的照射。
tā dài shàng mò jìng yǐ fáng qiáng guāng de zhào shè。
She put on dark glasses as a protection against the strong light.

她最喜爱的运动是滑雪, 其次是冰球.
tā zuì xǐ ài de yùn dòng shì huá xuě,  qí cì shì bīng qiú.
Next to skiing her favourite sport was ice-hockey.

她极力主张拼写正确是十分重要的.
tā jí lì zhǔ zhāng pīn xiě zhèng què shì shí fēn zhòng yào de.
She has very pronounced views on the importance of correct spelling.

她用灵巧的双手为我织了一副手套。
tā yòng líng qiǎo de shuāng shǒu wèi wǒ zhī le yī fù shǒu tào。
She knitted a pair of mittens for me with her nimble fingers.

她的活泼与兴高采烈的情绪把他迷住了.
tā de huó po yù xìng gāo cài liè de qíng xù bǎ tā mí zhù le.
He was charmed by her vivacity and high spirits.

她的美貌使她与其他女孩相比占了优势。
tā de měi mào shǐ tā yǔ qí tā nu:3 hái xiāng bǐ zhàn le yōu shì。
Her good look gave her a pull over other girls.

她离开小岛而在法国的大都市中成名。
tā lí kāi xiǎo dǎo ér zài fǎ guó de dà dū shì zhòng chéng míng。
She left the small island and became famous in metropolitan France.

她简化了指令以便于儿童理解。
tā jiǎn huà le zhǐ lìng yǐ biàn yú ér tóng lǐ jiě。
She simplified the instructions so that the children could understand them.

她给学会作了一次有关哲学的讲话.
tā jǐ xué huì zuò le yī cì yǒu guān zhé xué de jiǎng huà.
She delivered a talk on philosophy to the society.

她负责采购电视系列片所用的道具.
tā fù zé cǎi gòu diàn shì xì liè piān suǒ yòng de dào jù.
She was responsible for buying the properties for the television series.

她那些所谓的朋友对她的影响很坏.
tā nà xiē suǒ wèi de péng you duì tā de yǐng xiǎng hěn huài.
Those so-called friends of hers are a bad influence on her.

她那灵巧的手指把羊毛纺织成了细线。
tā nà líng qiǎo de shǒu zhǐ bǎ yáng máo fǎng zhī chéng le xì xiàn。
Her skillful fingers spun the wool out to a fine thread.

好看的身材或面貌上让人愉快的，端庄的
hǎo kàn de shēn cái huò miàn mào shàng ràng rén yú kuài de， duān zhuāng de
Pleasing and dignified in form or appearance.

如果要避开市中心，请从这里向右转弯。
rú guǒ yào bì kāi shì zhōng xīn， qǐng zòng zhè lǐ xiàng yòu zhuǎn wān。
To avoid the city center, turn right here.

学习植物学使我对大自然了解了许多。
xué xí zhí wù xué shǐ wǒ duì dà zì rán liǎo jiě le xǔ duō。
In learning botany, I understand much about nature.

孩子们在游泳池里互相把对方按入水中。
hái zi men zài yóu yǒng chí lǐ hù xiāng bǎ duì fāng àn rù shuǐ zhòng。
The children ducked each other in the swimming pool.

孩子们表演完后，大人们鼓掌。
hái zi men biǎo yǎn wán hòu， dà ren men gǔ zhǎng。
The grown-ups applauded after the children had finished their performance.

完整的茶具是在十八世纪发展起来的。

Complete tea services were developed in the 18th century.

寒冷的冬天，我们不得不穿毛织品。
hán lěng de dōng tiān， wǒ men bù dé bù chuān máo zhī pǐn。
We have to wear woolen clothes in the cold winter.

对他来说，生活似乎已失去了一切乐趣。
duì tā lái shuō， shēng huó sì hu yǐ shī qù le yī qiè lè qù。
Life seems to have lost most of its savor for him.

对我来说，拥有一辆汽车的花费太大。
duì wǒ lái shuō， yōng yǒu yī liàng qì chē de huā fèi tài dà。
It's too much of an expense for me to own a car.

尽管早上起来头疼，我还是照常上班。
jǐn guǎn zǎo shang qǐ lai tóu téng， wǒ hái shì zhào cháng shàng bān。
Although I got up with a headache, I went to work as usual.

局长坐在桌子一端她惯常坐的位置上。

The director took her accustomed place at the end of the table.

展现在我们面前的是一片广阔的土地。

A wide stretch of land spread in front of us.

工人们已经表明反对这些方案.
gōng rén men yǐ jīng biǎo míng fǎn duì zhè xie fāng àn.

市民们进行突击，试图冲破包围。

建筑费用涨到高达新台币两千万。

Building costs ran up to as much as NT$ 20 million.

开始做饭前，我还得去买些厨房用具。
kāi shǐ zuò fàn qián， wǒ huán de qù mǎi xiē chú fáng yòng jù。
I have to buy some kitchen utensils before starting cooking.

当地画家将要在这个风景点举办展览。
dāng dì huà jiā jiāng yào zài zhè gè fēng jǐng diǎn jǔ bàn zhǎn lǎn。
The local artists will hold an exhibition on the landmark.

当我们快到车站时，火车减慢了速度。

The train slackened speed as we approached the station.

影片中的声音必须与动作配合一致.

The sound on a film must synchronize with the action.

往来交往个人或群体间的交往或交际
wǎng lái jiāo wǎng gè rén huò qún tǐ jiàn de jiāo wǎng huò jiāo jì
Dealings or communications between persons or groups.

很少植物或动物能在沙漠中很好地生长。
hěn shǎo zhí wù huò dòng wù néng zài shā mò zhòng hěn hǎo de shēng zhǎng。
Few plants or animals thrive in the desert.

我不能再忍受他那傲慢无礼的行为了。
wǒ bù néng zài rěn shòu tā nà ào màn wú lǐ de xíng wéi le。
I could not endure the insolence of his behaviour.

我以为他要请客，但结果是各付各的。
wǒ yǐ wéi tā yào qǐng kè， dàn jié guǒ shì gè fù gè de。
I think he was treating, but it turned out to be a Dutch treat.

我们不得不把汽车拖到最近的修车厂。
wǒ men bù dé bù bǎ qì chē tuō dào zuì jìn de xiū jū chǎng。
We have to tow that car to the nearest garage.

我们不知道这些鸟如何找到它们的路。
wǒ men bù zhī dào zhè xie niǎo rú hé zhǎo dào tā men de lù。
We have no idea how the birds find their way.

我们为了双方的利益签订这项合同。
wǒ men wèi le shuāng fāng de lì yì qiān dìng zhè xiàng hé tong。
We entered into this contract in the interests of both parties.

我们全都是为了他才放弃这个计划的。
wǒ men quán dōu shì wèi le tā cái fàng qì zhè gè jì huà de。
It was all because of him that we gave up the plan.

我们公司是这个地区最大的用电户。
wǒ men gōng sī shì zhè gè dì qū zuì dà de yòng diàn hù。
Our company is the biggest user of electricity in this area.

我们发现可折叠的桌子使用非常方便。
wǒ men fā xiàn kě zhé dié de zhuō zi shǐ yòng fēi cháng fāng biàn。
We find our folding table a great convenience.

我们可以在话剧开演前一小时去取票.
wǒ men kě yǐ zài huà jù kāi yǎn qián yī xiǎo shí qù qǔ piào.
We can pick up the tickets an hour before the play begins.

我们听他们讲述撒哈拉沙漠的生活经历。
wǒ men tìng tā men jiǎng shù sǎ hǎ lā shā mò de shēng huó jīng lì。
We listened to their tales about life in the Sahara Desert.

我们复制了计算机磁盘以防意外。
wǒ men fù zhì le jì suàn jī cí pán yǐ fáng yì wài。
We make copies of our computer disks as a safeguard against accidents.

我们对医生这样对待我们感到不满。
wǒ men duì yī shēng zhè yàng duì dài wǒ men gǎn dào bù mǎn。
We are unhappy about the way the doctor treated us.

我们将怎样贯彻这个计划仍需要讨论。
wǒ men jiàng zěn yàng guàn chè zhè gè jì huà réng xū yào tǎo lùn。
How we shall carry out this plan still needs to be discussed.

我们希望能够和平过渡到新的制度。
wǒ men xī wàng néng gòu hé píng guò dù dào xīn de zhì dù。
We hope there will be a peaceful transition to the new system.

我们应充分利用丰富的人力资源。
wǒ men yìng chōng fèn lì yòng fēng fù de rén lì zī yuán。
We shall take full advantage of our rich source of human beings.

我们应该使用无烟煤以防止空气污染。
wǒ men yīng gāi shǐ yòng wú yān méi yǐ fáng zhǐ kōng qì wū rǎn。
We should use anthracite to avoid air pollution.

我们时间很紧, 只好胡乱吃了顿小吃.
wǒ men shí jiān hěn jǐn,  zhǐ hǎo hú luàn jí le dùn xiǎo chī.
We were in a hurry so we had to make do with a quick snack.

我们根据有效法律保护投资者的利益。
wǒ men gēn jù yǒu xiào fǎ lu:4 bǎo hù tóu zī zhě de lì yì。
We protect the interests of investors by the legislation in effect.

我们爬到山顶时, 看到了优美的景色.
wǒ men pá dào shān dǐng shí,  kàn dào le yōu měi de jǐng sè.
When we finally topped the hill we had a fine view.

我们现在正经历规模空前的失业现象。
wǒ men xiàn zài zhèng jing lì guī mó kōng qián de shī yè xiàn xiàng。
We are seeing unemployment on an unprecedented scale.

我们的副经理是公司的实际负责人。
wǒ men de fù jīng lǐ shì gōng sī de shí jì fù zé rén。
Our deputy manager is the virtual head of the business.

我们的教授要求他就这个课题写篇论文。
wǒ men de jiào shòu yāo qiú tā jiù zhè gè kè tí xiě piān lùn wén。
Our professor asked him to write a treatise on the subject.

我们的炮火控制了通往市区的各条道路。
wǒ men de pào huǒ kòng zhì le tōng wàng shì qū de gè tiáo dào lù。
Our guns covered every approach to the town.

我们的目标是进一步加强贸易关系。
wǒ men de mù biāo shì jìn yí bù jiā qiáng mào yì guān xi。
Our object is to further cement trade relations.

我们都同意他对政治形势的深刻分析。
wǒ men dōu tóng yì tā duì zhèng zhì xíng shì de shēn kè fēn xī。
We agreed with his acute analysis of the political situation.

我们须在我们日常公务中建立一些制度.
wǒ men xū zài wǒ men rì cháng gōng wù zhòng jiàn lì yī xiē zhì dù.
We must introduce some system into our office routine.

我们鼓励他坚持自己对此事的看法。
wǒ men gǔ lì tā jiān chí zì jǐ duì cǐ shì de kàn fǎ。
We encouraged him to assert his view of the matter.

我会陪在你身边，就象我答应你的那样。
wǒ kuài péi zài nǐ shēn biān， jiù xiàng wǒ dā ying nǐ de nà yàng。
I will be at your side, as I promised you.

我修改一下计划以便和你的计划相适应.
wǒ xiū gǎi yī xià jì huà yǐ biàn huò nǐ de jì huà xiàng shì yìng.
I will accommodate my plans to yours.

我假期在宾馆里干活儿，当服务员。
wǒ jià qī zài bīn guǎn lǐ gàn huó r， dàng fú wù yuán。
I got holiday jobs in guesthouses, waiting on tables.

我儿子生病时，丈夫给了我极大的安慰。
wǒ ér zi shēng bìng shí， zhàng fu jǐ le wǒ jí dà de ān wèi。
My husband was a great comfort to me when my son was ill.

我再也不想到这个糟糕的地方来了.
wǒ zài yě bù xiǎng dào zhè gè zāo gāo de dì fang lái le.
I have no intention of coming to this terrible place again!

我发现有人用过我的牙刷，我很不高兴。
wǒ fā xiàn yǒu rén yòng guò wǒ de yá shuā， wǒ hěn bù gāo xìng。
I am aggrieved to find that someone has used my toothbrush.

我叫她去刷牙, 她就跟我顶起嘴来.
wǒ jiào tā qù shuā yá,  tā jiù gēn wǒ dǐng qǐ zuǐ lái.
I asked her to go and brush her teeth and she just sassed me back.

我国任何时候都没有现在这样繁荣。
wǒ guó rèn hé shí hou dōu méi yǒu xiàn zài zhè yàng fán róng。
At no time has the country been more prosperous than at present.

我在一家非常富有创新精神的公司工作。
wǒ zài yī jiā fēi cháng fù yǒu chuàng xīn jīng shén de gōng sī gōng zuò。
I worked in a very innovative company.

我女儿喜欢给我讲她那些奇怪的梦。
wǒ nu:3 ér xǐ huan jǐ wǒ jiǎng tā nà xiē qí guài de mèng。
My daughter likes to describe her fantastic dreams to me.

我希望他不要将烟灰往地毯上乱弹。
wǒ xī wàng tā bù yào jiàng yān huī wàng dì tǎn shàng luàn tán。
I wish he would refrain from scattering his ash all over the carpet.

我想北极地区的人要比这里的少得多。
wǒ xiǎng běi jí dì qū de rén yào bì zhè lǐ de shào de duō。
I guess there are much less people in the Arctic regions than here.

我想征求一下你对这个计划的建议。
wǒ xiǎng zhēng qiú yī xià nǐ duì zhè gè jì huà de jiàn yì。
I should like to ask for your advice about the plan?

我愿意接受此品种，因为价格合理。
wǒ yuàn yì jiē shòu cǐ pǐn zhǒng， yīn wèi jià gé hé lǐ。
I'd like to accept this item, seeing (that) the price is reasonable.

我所有的业余时间都用在诗歌阅读上。
wǒ suǒ yǒu de yè yú shí jiān dōu yòng zài shī gē yuè dú shàng。
I spent all my spare time reading poetry.

我承认他身上有种强有力的优点。
wǒ chéng rèn tā shēn shàng yǒu zhòng qiáng yǒu lì de yōu diǎn。
I grant a sledge-hammering sort of merit in him.(Dickens)

我拿起了那把刀，把它扔到了窗外。
wǒ ná qǐ le nà bǎ dāo， bǎ tā rēng dào le chuāng wài。
I picked up the knife and threw it out of the window.

我插进了几则笑话，把我的讲话拉长了。
wǒ chā jìn le jǐ zé xiào huà， bǎ wǒ de jiǎng huà lā zhǎng le。
I made my speech longer by padding it with a few jokes.

我每天至少要把厨房地板擦洗一次。
wǒ měi tiān zhì shǎo yào bǎ chú fáng dì bǎn cā xǐ yī cì。
I have to mop the kitchen floor at least once a day.

我毫无保留地认为他说的是实话。
wǒ háo wú bǎo liú de rèn wéi tā shuō de shì shí huà。
I accepted without reservation what he had said as true.

我相信礼貌对大家是很重要的。
wǒ xiāng xìn lǐ mào duì dà jiā shì hěn zhòng yào de。
It is my belief that good manners are very important to everybody.

我答应一定完好无损地还你的自行车。
wǒ dā ying yī dìng wán hǎo wú sǔn de huán nǐ de zì xíng chē。
I promise to return your bicycle on good condition.

我要去购物，因为我需要买些日用品。
wǒ yào qù gòu wù， yīn wèi wǒ xū yào mǎi xiē rì yòng pǐn。
I'm going shopping because I need to buy some daily necessities.

我觉得这是个合理的建议，但他不同意。
wǒ jué de zhè shì gè hé lǐ de jiàn yì， dàn tā bù tóng yì。
I thought it was a reasonable proposal, but he didn't agree.

我认为能被邀请参加晚宴是很大的荣幸。
wǒ rèn wéi néng bèi yāo qǐng cān jiā wǎn yàn shì hěn dà de róng xìng。
I consider it a great honor to be invited to dinner.

我设法自立而不求助于我的父母。
wǒ shè fǎ zì lì ér bù qiú zhù yú wǒ de fù mǔ。
I tried to stand on my own two feet rather than turned to my parents.

我负担不起带花园的大房子的维护费.
wǒ fù dān bù qǐ dài huā yuán de dà fáng zi de wéi hù fèi.
I can't afford the upkeep of a large house and garden.

我跟太太争论有关家庭费用的问题。
wǒ gēn tài tai zhēng lùn yǒu guān jiā tíng fèi yòng de wèn tí。
I disputed with my wife on household expenses.

我还没来得及给他盖好被子，他就睡着了。
wǒ huán mò lái de jí jǐ tā gě hào bèi zi， tā jiù shuì zhāo le。
He was asleep before I tucked him in.

我连移动双脚的力气都几乎没有了。
wǒ lián yí dòng shuāng jué de lì qi dōu jī hū méi yǒu le。
I have hardly enough strength left to move my feet.

我通过职业介绍所找到了这份工作。
wǒ tōng guò zhí yè jiè shào suǒ zhǎo dào le zhè fèn gōng zuò。
I got this job through an employment agency.

或许这些营养品对你的健康有帮助。
huò xǔ zhè xie yíng yǎng pǐn duì nǐ de jiàn kāng yǒu bāng zhù。
Maybe these nutrients are helpful to your health.

战争带来的必然结果就是生产力下降。
zhàn zhēng dài lái de bì rán jié guǒ jiù shì shēng chǎn lì xià jiàng。
The necessary outcome of a war is a fall in production.

手术成功了，病人现在已脱离危险。
shǒu shù chéng gōng le， bìng rén xiàn zài yǐ tuō lí wēi xiǎn。
The operation is a success and now the patient is out of danger.

把发生的事情尽可能仔细地回忆一下.
bǎ fā shēng de shì qing jìn kě néng zǐ xì de huí yì yī xià.
Try to recall (to mind) exactly what happened.

护理工作既是职业又是救死扶伤的责任。
hù lǐ gōng zuò jì shì zhí yè yòu shì jiù sǐ fú shāng de zé rèn。
Nursing is a vocation as well as a profession.

抬起这只沉重的箱子要花费相当大的力气。
tái qǐ zhè zhǐ chén zhòng de xiāng zǐ yào huā fèi xiāng dāng dà de lì qi。
It's quite an effort to lift this heavy box.

担任主席的人有责任安排会议。
dān rèn zhǔ xí de rén yǒu zé rèn ān pái huì yì。
The holder of the office of chairman is responsible for arranging meetings.

拥有世界冠军是我们每个公民的骄傲。
yōng yǒu shì jiè guàn jūn shì wǒ men měi gè gōng mín de jiāo ào。
It's a civic pride to have a champion.

拥有汽车的人数一直在逐渐上升。
yōng yǒu qì chē de rén shù yī zhí zài zhú jiàn shàng shēng。
There has been a gradual increase in the number of people owning cars.

按学生人数, 我们应该建三个餐厅。
àn xué sheng rén shù,  wǒ men yīng gāi jiàn sān gè cān tīng。
In proportion to the number of students we should build 3 dining rooms.

据目前情况看，我们不能按时完成任务了。
jù mù qián qíng kuàng kàn， wǒ men bù néng àn shí wán chéng rèn wu le。
As things stand, we won't finish the job on time.

接替他担任主席的人将参加本次会议。
jiē tì tā dān rèn zhǔ xí de rén jiàng cān jiā běn cì huì yì。
His successor as the chairman will be at the conference.

搬运工会把你的行李搬到你的房间去的。
bān yùn gōng huì bǎ nǐ de xíng li bān dào nǐ de fáng jiān qù de。
The porter will carry your luggage to your room.

改革教育制度将是一个艰难的过程.
gǎi gé jiào yù zhì dù jiàng shì yī gè jiān nán de guò chéng.
Reforming the education system will be a difficult process.

政府不允许报道那起严重事故。
zhèng fǔ bù yǔn xǔ bào dào nà qǐ yán zhòng shì gù。
The government didn't allow reporting the terrible accident.

政府不应浪费资金去扶持那些无望的企业.
zhèng fǔ bù yìng làng fèi zī jīn qù fú chí nà xiē wú wàng de qǐ yè.
The government should not waste money supporting lame ducks.

政府对工会表现得越来越不耐烦。
zhèng fǔ duì gōng huì biǎo xiàn de yuè lái yuè bù nài fán。
The governments showed growing impatience at the unions.

政府对引进科学设备非常感兴趣。
zhèng fǔ duì yǐn jìn kē xué shè bèi fēi cháng gǎn xìng qu。
The government has an interest in importing scientific equipment.

政府已答应采取措施来帮助失业者。
zhèng fǔ yǐ dā ying cǎi qǔ cuò shī lái bāng zhù shī yè zhě。
The government has promised to take measures to help the unemployed.

政府计画严格限制今年公费开支.
zhèng fǔ jì huà yán gé xiàn zhì jīn nián gōng fèi kāi zhī.
The government plans to set strict limits on public spending this year.

敌人的防线很坚强, 但仍为我军突破。
dí rén de fáng xiàn hěn jiān qiáng,  dàn réng wèi wǒ jūn tū pò。
The enemy's defenses were strong but our soldiers broke through.

教师给我们每个人都分配了假日的工作.
jiào shī jǐ wǒ men měi gè rén dōu fēn pèi le jià rì de gōng zuò.
The teacher has assigned each of us a holiday task.

教授将要做关于地理特征的讲座。
jiào shòu jiāng yào zuò guān yú dì lǐ tè zhēng de jiǎng zuò。
The professor will give a lecture of geographical features.

整个计划开始具有更切合实际的性质。
zhěng gè jì huà kāi shǐ jù yǒu gèng qiè hé shí jì de xìng zhì。
The whole scheme began to take on a more practical aspect.

新任命的将军立即向敌人发起攻击.
xīn rèn mìng de jiāng jūn lì jí xiàng dí rén fā qǐ gōng jī.
The new general immediately launched an offensive against the enemy.

新政府的成立带来了一个繁荣的时期.
xīn zhèng fǔ de chéng lì dài lái le yī gè fán róng de shí qī.
The new government ushered in a period of prosperity.

既然你坚持，我就只好修改信用证。
jì rán nǐ jiān chí， wǒ jiù zhǐ hǎo xiū gǎi xìn yòng zhèng。
Since you insist, I must amend the letter of credit.

既然她病得厉害, 我们要马上去请医生。
jì rán tā bìng de lì hai,  wǒ men yào mǎ shàng qù qǐng yī shēng。
Since she is seriously ill, we have to send for a doctor at once.

明年将要修建一条超级高速公路。
míng nián jiāng yào xiū jiàn yī tiáo chāo jí gāo sù gōng lù。
A superhighway will be constructed next year.

最后，我终于成功地让我的车子慢慢移动。
zuì hòu， wǒ zhōng yú chéng gōng de ràng wǒ de jū zi màn màn yí dòng。
At last I succeeded in getting my car moving slowly.

最近有关离婚的电视剧太多了。
zuì jìn yǒu guān lí hūn de diàn shì jù tài duō le。
There has been a surfeit of plays about divorce on the TV recently.

有一个省脱离了旧政府而另组新政府。
yǒu yī gè xǐng tuō lí le jiù zhèng fǔ ér lìng zǔ xīn zhèng fǔ。
A province has broken away to form a new state.

有一点是肯定的, 你再也不能行走了.
yǒu yī diǎn shì kěn dìng de,  nǐ zài yě bù néng xíng zǒu le.
This much is certain, you will never walk again.

有个学生真冒失, 竟然和教授争论起来.
yǒu gè xué sheng zhēn mào shī,  jìng rán huò jiào shòu zhēng lùn qǐ lai.
One student made so bold as to argue with the professor.

有些食物比另一些食物容易吸收.
yǒu xiē shí wù bì lìng yī xiē shí wù róng yì xī shōu.
Some foods assimilate/ are assimilated more easily than others.

有些食物的吸收比另一些更容易。
yǒu xiē shí wù de xī shōu bì lìng yī xiē gèng róng yì。
The assimilation of some foods is more easily than that of others.

有关环境的会议将在下周一举行。
yǒu guān huán jìng de huì yì jiàng zài xià zhōu yī jǔ xíng。
The convocation about environment will be held on next Monday.

有前面那个人挡著, 我看不见球赛.
yǒu qián mian nèi gè rén dàng著,  wǒ kàn bù jiàn qiú sài.
The man in front was obstructing my view of the pitch.

本世纪我们已经经历了两次世界大战。
běn shì jì wǒ men yǐ jīng jīng lì le liǎng cì shì jiè dà zhàn。
We have had two world wars in this century.

本身行为不正, 则不宜批评别人.
běn shēn xíng wéi bù zhèng,  zé bù yí pī píng bié rén.
You can ill afford to criticize others when you behave so badly yourself.

本阅览室的参考书不得私自带出。
běn yuè lǎn shì de cān kǎo shū bù dé sī zì dài chū。
No reference books are to be taken out of the reading room without permission.

村子的礼堂专作举行庆典和会议之用.
cūn zi de lǐ táng zhuān zuò jǔ xíng qìng diǎn huò huì yì zhī yòng.
The village hall is given over to civic functions and meetings.

查一下火车时刻表中下一趟车的时间.
zhā yī xià huǒ chē shí kè biǎo zhòng xià yī tàng jū de shí jiān.
Look up the time of the next train in the timetable.

根据表面现象看问题有时是不可取的。
gēn jù biǎo miàn xiàn xiàng kàn wèn tí yǒu shí shì bù kě qǔ de。
It's not always wise to go by appearances.

植物从泥土中吸收矿物质和其他养料。
zhí wù zòng ní tǔ zhòng xī shōu kuàng wù zhì huò qí tā yǎng liào。
Plants absorb minerals and other nutrients from the soil.

每月都从运河中打捞出几辆旧汽车来.
měi yuè dōu zòng yùn hé zhòng dǎ lāo chū jǐ liàng jiù qì chē lái.
Several old cars are fished out (of the canal) every month.

毕业前，我们会接受一些职业训练。
bì yè qián， wǒ men kuài jiē shòu yī xiē zhí yè xùn liàn。
We will have some vocational training before graduation.

民间音乐是一代一代地流传下来的。
mín jiān yīn yuè shì yī dài yī dài de liú chuán xia lai de。
Folk music has been passed down from one generation to another.

汽车在离墙不到一英寸的地方停住了。
qì chē zài lí qiáng bù dào yī yīng cùn de dì fang tíng zhù le。
The car stopped within a fraction of an inch of the wall.

没料到，他对这件事的反应是这样的。
mò liào dào， tā duì zhè jiàn shì de fǎn yìng shì zhè yàng de。
His reaction on this matter is unexpected.

海关官员根本没检查我们的行李。
hǎi guān guān yuán gēn běn mò jiǎn chá wǒ men de xíng li。
The Customs officer didn't bother to check our luggage.

游击队在那个省开辟了一条新战线。
yóu jī duì zài nèi gè xǐng kāi pì le yī tiáo xīn zhàn xiàn。
The guerrillas opened up a new front in that province.

环保部门要求我们使用无烟煤。
huán bǎo bù mén yāo qiú wǒ men shǐ yòng wú yān méi。
We are required by environment protecting department to use anthracite.

现实中, 事情总是出乎意料地发生。
xiàn shí zhòng,  shì qing zǒng shì chū hū yì liào de fā shēng。
In reality, things always happen out of expectation.

现实生活并不象人们想象的那样美好。
xiàn shí shēng huó bìng bù xiàng rén men xiǎng xiàng de nà yàng měi hǎo。
Real life isn't as happy as people imagine.

现行的教育制度和现实并不一致。
xiàn xíng de jiào yù zhì dù huò xiàn shí bìng bù yī zhì。
The current education system is not in concert with the reality.

生命可以被比作一次不知目的地的旅行。
shēng mìng kě yǐ bèi bì zuò yī cì bù zhī mù dì dì de lu:3 xíng。
Life can be likened to a journey with an unknown destination.

生活费用上升，老年人最受影响。
shēng huó fèi yòng shàng shēng， lǎo nián rén zuì shòu yǐng xiǎng。
Old people are hardest hit by the rising cost of living.

由上面所说的，我们可以做一个结论。

紫禁城是世界上最伟大的建筑之一。
zǐ jìn chéng shì shì jiè shàng zuì wěi dà de jiàn zhù zhī yī。
The Forbidden City is one of the world's greatest works of architecture.

经济知识对于理解这个问题是至关重要的。

老师从一开始就强调翻译准确性。
lǎo shī zòng yī kāi shǐ jiù qiáng diào fān yì zhǔn què xìng。

老师的办公室里堆满了大批不同的论文。

虽然任务艰巨，他们还是设法及时完成。
suī rán rèn wu jiān jù， tā men hái shì shè fǎ jí shí wán chéng。

表否定的将一个词的意义由肯定变为否定的
biǎo fǒu dìng de jiàng yī gè cí de yì yì yóu kěn dìng biàn wèi fǒu dìng de
Altering the meaning of a term from positive to negative.

被围困在城里的老百姓已空运到安全地区.

要洗的衣物须称过重量再放入洗衣机中.

让我看看买卖这块土地的所有官方文件。

试验没有成功，尽管如此，还是值得做的。

诗人表达了他对所爱的女子火一般的激情。

这三个人根据各自的能力被分配了工作。

这两个国家因为外交争端即将开战。

这两样东西外表相同，但本质上却不样。

这个小女孩太可爱了，我把她叫做小精灵。
